<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_e9f5f1fe-7fdb-44e8-a685-b52a73a43b79'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer12494289552797067007">I was trying to read a book on my kindle, but because of the format, I had to stop reading it to read this one. Sighing. It's not like I am a newbie with my kindle. I've used it for several years now. However, even after reading the kindle instructions, which were very clear, I was unable to read the former book in an easy fashion. It has to be tweaked several ways because somehow the previous book's format simply does not work with my paperwhite kindle. I will read the book, but I had hoped to </span>
  <span id="freeText12494289552797067007" style="display:none">I was trying to read a book on my kindle, but because of the format, I had to stop reading it to read this one. Sighing. It's not like I am a newbie with my kindle. I've used it for several years now. However, even after reading the kindle instructions, which were very clear, I was unable to read the former book in an easy fashion. It has to be tweaked several ways because somehow the previous book's format simply does not work with my paperwhite kindle. I will read the book, but I had hoped to find a solution making it a joy to read rather than a pain in the bum.</span>

<div id="review_1561378893" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1561378893" />
    <a title="Tyler McGlothlin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/46498084-tyler-mcglothlin"><img alt="Tyler McGlothlin" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1561378893?book_show_action=true">Feb 26, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tyler McGlothlin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tyler McGlothlin" href="/user/show/46498084-tyler-mcglothlin">Tyler McGlothlin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23149625-gu-a-del-usuario-de-kindle-paperwhite">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1561378893" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9761864521567824252">Pretty good book. I felt like I was there. I can not see Janet being realistic, she just seems like she is too crazy to be relatable to. I did like how the author decided to kill off Janet at the end. She was really bringing me down along with the rest of the characters. I hope she doesn't come back in the next book or else I will probably stop reading this series.<br/><br/>-Tyler</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3576517890" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3576517890" />
    <a title="Julian Chiu" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/121572978-julian-chiu"><img alt="Julian Chiu" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/m_50x66-82093808bca726cb3249a493fbd3bd0f.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3576517890?book_show_action=true">Oct 01, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Julian Chiu" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Julian Chiu" href="/user/show/121572978-julian-chiu">Julian Chiu</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/53498056-kindle-paperwhite-user-s-guide">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer3576517890&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3576517890" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9256171617727860651">Great character development throughout the book, this is something more than a user manual, it is actually something way more meaningful than that, I’ve stared at the book cover for 5 hours now, and I think I just understood how this is the most important book for a new kindle user. Starting with the cover design, there is simply nothing aesthetically pleasing about it, it’s just a square box with the title inside, heck even the square isn’t pretty, it is a square inside a rectangle screen makin</span>
  <span id="freeText9256171617727860651" style="display:none">Great character development throughout the book, this is something more than a user manual, it is actually something way more meaningful than that, I’ve stared at the book cover for 5 hours now, and I think I just understood how this is the most important book for a new kindle user. Starting with the cover design, there is simply nothing aesthetically pleasing about it, it’s just a square box with the title inside, heck even the square isn’t pretty, it is a square inside a rectangle screen making it sticking out in a weird way. But, a user manual doesn’t need a nice looking cover, just the bare title is required for the manual, and the author even took the time to add in a ‘4th Edition’ at the bottom as a way to make it seem more interesting for both newcomers and the ones who’ve seen the 3rd edition.<br /><br />In the table of contents, it thoroughly covers out the basics and advanced usages of the kindle paperwhite, such as how to override the current settings to get 4K display of the wordings. The author also clearly indicated that this device is also a tool for Amazon to run it’s ads for the countless users, which kind of sucks because even though you are buying a special device that is designed just for reading, you would still be monitored by the algorithm on your favourite genre, average time to finish a book, and time spent on it everyday to calculate which books to recommend to you, and if it doesn’t work, it would switch to another one and eventually you give in and click on the ‘recommended’ and buy whatever the advertisers want you to. Although there is a option to remove ads for 20 USD, it is not easy to find the option within the settings, as amazon can clearly benefit more from the advertisers than the 20 USD you paid.<br /><br /><br /><br />The chapters are also evenly divided by how important each part is for Amazon, from starting off letting you know your monitored by them, to showing you how to buy their advertised books by scrolling down, which is easier to access than to go online to find a book, and then typing out the book name in the search bar, how convenient! <br /><br /><br />After reading the entire manual, I am authorised to tell every new kindle users to give this book a try before purchasing anything, as it could give you a through understanding of how the device works, and how it is working for Amazon.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9256171617727860651" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2605908818" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2605908818" />
    <a title="Bonnie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1679313-bonnie"><img alt="Bonnie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1364082932p2/1679313.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2605908818?book_show_action=true">Feb 28, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bonnie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bonnie" href="/user/show/1679313-bonnie">Bonnie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2605908818" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11202598559203654963">There were some things I didn't understand about the latest Kindle software so I checked out this book. It wasn't all that useful and I mostly figured things out by myself.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('0qHBZRsPQ1xAV0HWwqlfqEsE43caJ5TC4xEcnPSiKHbxNGveimYgfZsHJOG8qVMMyeN1iRcBPbj8/rPU6uEY7g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {

  }
